***ras.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ras.html>ras</a> (3260)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">race</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ras.html>ras</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rassen.html>rassen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ras.html>rasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">race</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">breed</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rasch</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rasc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*raskuz</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">rash</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">rasch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ras.html>ras</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ras.html>rasser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ras.html>ras</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">rast</b>)
</p>

***ratatouille.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ratatouille.html>ratatouille</a> (43167)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Learned borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:ratatouille.html>ratatouille</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Occitan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Occitan language">Occitan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="oc">ratatolha</i>. The French <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> analysable as a derivative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">touiller</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stir</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tudiculare</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grind, to mix</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of the popular borrowing <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ratjetoe</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ratatouille.html>ratatouille</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ratatouille.html>ratatouilles</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ratatouille.html>ratatouille</a></span>: a traditional French Provençal stewed vegetable dish consisting primarily of tomatoes, <a href = vnd.unilang:zucchini.html>zucchini</a> and eggplant, with other ingredients.</li></ol>
<p><br clear="all" />
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ratelen.html>ratele</a></i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ratel.html>ratel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ratels.html>ratels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ratel.html>rateltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">ratchet</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">rattle</span></li>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">socket wrench</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">rattle</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">organ for making noise, such as a rattlesnake's</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***ratelslang.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ratelslang.html>ratelslang</a> (17982)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ratel.html>ratel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rattle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">snake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">rattlesnake</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ratelslang.html>ratelslang</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ratelslangen.html>ratelslangen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ratelslang.html>ratelslangetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">rattlesnake</span> (poisonous snake with a rattling tail), snake of the genera <i>Crotalus</i> or <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Sistrurus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Sistrurus"><i>Sistrurus</i></a></span></li></ol>

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rou</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">raeu</i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:roo.html>roo</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:rao.html>rao</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrawaz</i>.

***ravel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ravel.html>ravel</a> (59483)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ravelen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to tangle, fray out, unweave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rafel.html>rafel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">frayed thread</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ravel.html>ravel</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">ravels</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A snarl; a complication.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1927</b>,  DH Lawrence,  <cite>Mornings in Mexico</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://gutenberg.net.au/ebooks09/0900391h.html">[1]</a></sup>, HTML edition, Project Gutenberg Australia, published <i>2009</i>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The <a href = vnd.unilang:savannah.html>savannah</a> valley <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> shadeless, spotted only with the thorny <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ravel.html>ravel</a></b> of <a href = vnd.unilang:mesquite.html>mesquite</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bushes.html>bushes</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A ravelled thread.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ravel.html>ravel</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">ravels</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">ravelling</b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">raveling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">ravelled</b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">raveled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To tangle; entangle; entwine confusedly, become snarled; thus to involve; perplex; confuse.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by <a href = vnd.unilang:waller.html>Waller</a> and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>What glory's due to him that could divide / Such <b>ravelled</b> interests?</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Jeremy <a href = vnd.unilang:taylor.html>Taylor</a> and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>The faith of very many <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> seems a duty so weak and indifferent, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> so often untwisted by violence, or <b>ravelled</b> and entangled in weak discourses!</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1871</b>,  <cite>Popular Science News</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=9hpbAAAAYAAJamp;pg=PA61amp;lpg=PA61amp;dq=%22Minute+glands,+which+resemble+ravelled+tubes,%22amp;source=blamp;ots=Sjz9CS7rIBamp;sig=BY1JSsEQLrBtarbOHNSaBwPmhIwamp;hl=enamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22Minute%20glands%2C%20which%20resemble%20ravelled%20tubes%2C%22amp;f=false">[2]</a></sup>, volume 5-7, Digitized edition, published <i>2011</i>, page 61:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">… and in them are minute <i>glands</i>, which resemble <b>ravelled</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:tubes.html>tubes</a> …</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> September 10,  Martha <a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>. Moore,  “After 9/11, dinner <a href = vnd.unilang:gang.html>gang</a> raises funds to honor those lost”, in  <cite>USA Today</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.usatoday.com/news/nation/story/2011-09-08/911-friends-dinner-first-thursday/50337710/1?csp=34news">[3]</a></sup>, retrieved <span class="mw-formatted-date" title="2012-08-24">2012-08-24</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">But the real work of the First Thursday Foundation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> remembering, and its biggest gift <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> knitting back together <a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>lives</a> <b>raveled</b> by loss.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To undo the intricacies of; to disentangle or clarify.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To pull apart (especially cloth or a seam); unravel.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To become entangled.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To become untwisted or unwoven.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> programming</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> In the APL programming language, to reshape (a variable) into a vector.
<ul><li><b>1975</b>, Tse-yun Feng, <i>Parallel processing: proceedings of the Sagamore Computer Conference</i>
<dl><dd>LOAD.S loads a sequence of scalars from the <b>ravelled</b> form of a matrix into successive AM elements.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1980</b>,  Gijsbert <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:linden.html>Linden</a>,  <cite>APL 80: International Conference on APL, June 24-26, 1980</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><b>Ravelling</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> necessary because the execute function in the IBM implementation only accepts charactervectors as argument.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The spellings <i>ravelling</i> and <i>ravelled</i> are more common in the UK than in the US.</li></ul>
</body>

***raw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> raw (2992)</h1><br></body> 
***rawhide.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rawhide.html>rawhide</a> (56190)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">raw</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hide</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rawhide.html>rawhide</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">rawhides</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Untanned hide.
<ul><li><b>1907</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/O._Henry" class="extiw" title="w:O. Henry"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a></a>, <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Hearts_and_Crosses" class="extiw" title="s:Hearts and Crosses">"<a href = vnd.unilang:hearts.html>Hearts</a> and Crosses"</a>:
<dl><dd>This throw <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> fair; the white cow <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> to earth again; and before it could rise Santa <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> made the <a href = vnd.unilang:lasso.html>lasso</a> fast around a post of the corral with a swift and simple knot, and <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> leaped upon the cow again with the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rawhide.html>rawhide</a></b> hobbles.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A whip made from twisted untanned leather.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rawhide.html>rawhide</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">rawhides</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">rawhiding</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">rawhided</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To clear (a pump) of sediment by starting and stopping it repeatedly.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To beat with a <a href = vnd.unilang:rawhide.html>rawhide</a> whip.</li></ol>
</body>

***razzia.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:razzia.html>razzia</a> (56187)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i>razia</i> (1830), borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algerian_Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Algerian Arabic">Algerian Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="arq">غَزِيَّة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="arq-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ḡaziya</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, classical Arabic <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">غَزْوَة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ḡazwa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">raid, military campaign</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">gazia</i>.
</p><p><span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> raid <span class="defdate">[from 1840s]</span></li></ol>

***reaper.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:reaper.html>reaper</a> (17592)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">reper</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">repare</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">repere</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">*riper</i> (the last, attested only in surnames <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">Ryper</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">Riper</i>, etc.), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">rīpere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:reaper.html>reaper</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">reap</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:reaper.html>reaper</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:reapers.html>reapers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One who reaps.</li>
<li>A machine used to harvest crops.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often with initial capital</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Short for <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Grim <a href = vnd.unilang:reaper.html>Reaper</a></i></span></span>.
<ul><li><b>1976</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Buck_Dharma" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Buck Dharma">Buck Dharma</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Blue_%C3%96yster_Cult" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Blue Öyster Cult">Blue Öyster Cult</a>), "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Don%27t_Fear_the_Reaper" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Don | t Fear the Reaper">Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> Fear the <a href = vnd.unilang:reaper.html>Reaper</a></a>" (song)
<dl><dd>Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> fear the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:reaper.html>Reaper</a></b> / <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> be able to fly</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1999</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:karl.html>Karl</a> S. Guthke, <i>The Gender of Death: A Cultural History in Art and Literature</i> (page 7)
<dl><dd>Why <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the Grim <a href = vnd.unilang:reaper.html>Reaper</a> a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>? True, the noun ending would theoretically allow us to visualize the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:reaper.html>reaper</a></b> as a woman as well, but <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">reap</span></li></ul>
</body>

***reason.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> reason (350)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
